Actor Goldeneye_PartBase
{
	Radius 14
	Height 52
	+NOINTERACTION
	+THRUACTORS
	+NODROPOFF
	+FLOORCLIP
	+CLIENTSIDEONLY
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			GE00 A 0
			GE00 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("GoldeneyePartPositioner")
			GE00 A 1
		Spawn2:
		NoWhere:
			GE00 ABCDEFGHIJIHGFEDCB 6
			Loop
		Walking:
			GE06 ABCDEFGHIJ 6
			Loop
		SpawnDual:
			GE84 ABCDEFGHIJKLMLKJIHGFEDCB 6
			Loop
		IdleAdjustCrotch:
			GE01 ABCDEFGHIJ 6
			Goto Spawn2

Actor Goldeneye_LaserRayEnemy : Goldeneye_BulletTracer
{
	Damage(CallACS("Goldeneye_TracerDamage"))
	+THRUACTORS
	RenderStyle Translucent
    States
    {
        Spawn:
			GE00 A 0
			TNT1 A 1
			GE00 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(velx*2,vely*2,velz*2,CVF_REPLACE)
		SpawnLoop:
			GE00 A 0 A_Explode(CallACS("Goldeneye_TracerDamage"), 8, !XF_HURTSOURCE, false, 8)
            GE00 A 1 Bright
            loop
        Death:
            TNT1 A 0 A_Playsound("Goldeneye/Zap", CHAN_5)
            TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Goldeneye_Debris", frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-1, 1), frandom(-360, 360), SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Goldeneye_BulletImpact", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
            TNT1 A 0
            Stop
			}
}

{

	Projectile
	Height 8

			GE00 Z 0 A_SetPitch(random(0,360))
		SpawnLoop:
			GE00 Z 0 A_SetPitch(pitch-15)

			GE00 Z -1
			Stop
		}

Actor Goldeneye_PP7EnemyDrop : AmmoBackpack //fake backpack. Gives the rewards a backpack would normally give, but does not expand ammo capacity
{
	Gravity 0.33
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Found a PP7 and some ammo!"
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			GE00 Z 0
			GE00 Z 0 ThrustThing(random(0,256)/360,random(1,2),0,0)
			GE00 Z 0 ThrustThingZ(0,random(0,2),0,0)
			GE00 Z 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,360))
			GE00 Z 0 A_SetPitch(random(0,360))
		SpawnLoop:
			GE00 Z 0 A_SetPitch(pitch-15)
			GE00 Z 0 A_SetAngle(angle-15)
			GE00 Z 0 A_CheckFloor("FloorLoop")		
			GE00 Z 1
			Loop
		FloorLoop:
			GE00 A 0 A_PlaySound("Goldeneye/DropLand", CHAN_BODY, 1.5)
			GE00 A 0 A_Stop
			GE00 A 0 A_SetPitch(0)		
			GE00 Z -1
			Stop
		Pickup:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MarathonClass", 1, "PickupMarathon")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("HexenClass", 1, "PickupHexen")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("WolfenClass", 1, "PickupWolfen")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BondClass", 1, "PickupBond")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("CatacombClass", 1, "PickupCatacomb")
//			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("WitchavenClass", 0, "PickupWitchaven")	Why?
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Goldeneye/Weaponup")
			TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 10)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Shell", 4)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("RocketAmmo", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Cell", 20)
			stop	
		PickupWitchaven:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Goldeneye/Weaponup")
			TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 20)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Shell", 8)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("RocketAmmo", 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Cell", 40)
			stop
		PickupWolfen:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Goldeneye/Weaponup")
			TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 20)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("RocketAmmo", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Cell", 20)
			stop	
		PickupMarathon:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("marathon/itemget")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetBlend("Green", 0.4, 4)
			TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 10)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Shell", 4)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("RocketAmmo", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Cell", 20)
			stop
		PickupBond:
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Goldeneye_PP7DualToken", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Goldeneye/Weaponup")
			TNT1 A 1 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 10)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Shell", 4)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("RocketAmmo", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Cell", 20)
			stop	
	    PickupCatacomb:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Catacomb/ItemGet3")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_XTerminators", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_Zappers", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_Nukes", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_LargeHealthPotion", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_Bursts", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_Bolts", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Catacomb_Waves", Random(0,3))
			TNT1 A 0
			stop					
	}
}

			GE00 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,random(0,1),0,0)
			GE00 A 0 A_SetAngle(random(0,360))
			GE00 A 0 A_SetPitch(random(0,360))

			GE00 A 0 A_SetPitch(pitch-15)

			GE00 A 0 A_CheckFloor("Death")
			GE00 A 2
			Loop
		Death:
			GE00 A 0 A_Stop
			GE00 A 0 A_SetPitch(0)

			GE00 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 2 A_FadeOut(0.05)
			Stop
	}

Actor Goldeneye_EnemyGrenade
{
	Damage(0)
	Projectile
	Height 8
	Radius 4
	Speed 8
	-NOGRAVITY
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+EXTREMEDEATH
	Gravity 0.5
	Scale 0.75
	DeathSound "Goldeneye/Explosion"
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			GE00 A 0
			GE00 A 0 A_ChangeVelocity(0,0,8,CVF_RELATIVE)
			GE00 A 0 A_SetPitch(random(0,360))
		SpawnLoop:
			GE00 A 1 A_SetPitch(pitch+15)
			loop
		Death:
